  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_07497e75-5fc4-4970-bc63-b3a34394b182'
      });
    }

  <span id="freeText6284153988653760919" style="display:none">Two strangers...<br /><br />When accountant Makenna James finds herself stranded in a pitch-black elevator, she can't help but wonder about the stranger stuck with her. All she noticed about him before the lights went out was a dragon tattoo; all she knows now is his sexy, gruff voice in the darkness. <br /><br />Four hours...<br /><br />Caden Grayson is inked, pierced, scarred on the inside and out—and terrified of the dark for reasons he'd rather not remember. Trapped in his worst nightmare, only the sweet voice of the red-headed beauty distracts him from his fear. And, oh, man, as the hours pass and the darkness heats up, that's nothing compared to her touch.<br /><br />One pitch-black elevator...<br /><br />He's all rough edges and she's pin-striped skirts, but in the darkness they open up and reach out without any preconceptions to hold them back. But as attraction grows and sparks fly, will they feel the same when the lights come back on?<br /><br /><br />The Hearts in Darkness Duet Continues with LOVE IN THE LIGHT!</span>

<div id="review_200910833" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/200910833" />
    <a title="Kristen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen"><img alt="Kristen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1312922334p2/5477946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/200910833?book_show_action=true">Aug 21, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristen" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen">Kristen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/11258847-hearts-in-darkness">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=tattooed-pierced-hero">tattooed-pierced-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=scrumptious-hero">scrumptious-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=favorite-books">favorite-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=novella-short-story">novella-short-story</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer200910833" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16830297584220961979"><b>Huge 5 stars.</b><br/><br/><i>Hearts In Darkness</i> is one of those stories that touches your heart, makes you ponder and leaves a smile on your face for the rest of the day.<br/><br/>The novella begins with two people whose outward appearance is as different as night and day. Makenna is stylish, tailored, attractive, and well-groomed, albeit slightly frazzled. On the other hand, Caden is a nonconformist with tattoos, piercings, and a shaved head. Within seconds of Makenna entering an elevator that Caden was already in, the </span>
  <span id="freeText16830297584220961979" style="display:none"><b>Huge 5 stars.</b><br /><br /><i>Hearts In Darkness</i> is one of those stories that touches your heart, makes you ponder and leaves a smile on your face for the rest of the day.<br /><br />The novella begins with two people whose outward appearance is as different as night and day. Makenna is stylish, tailored, attractive, and well-groomed, albeit slightly frazzled. On the other hand, Caden is a nonconformist with tattoos, piercings, and a shaved head. Within seconds of Makenna entering an elevator that Caden was already in, the elevator stops, the lights go out, and the two are left together in the dark. Neither has had an opportunity to get more than a glimpse of the other. What ensues is a touching, emotional, and highly sensual connection between two people who find they admire each other and have much in common because they are not bound by preconceived notions that all too often blind us all.<br /><br />The author had the ability to easily transport me into Makenna’s and Caden’s world. I loved their banter, their insecurities, their erotically charged chemistry, and their honesty. In short, I was highly invested in this book’s wonderful but complex characters and in their emotional and extremely sensual story. <br /><br />I loved everything about this sweet but highly erotic book. I wholeheartedly recommend it.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16830297584220961979" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer14382065105596110892">5 stars – Contemporary Romance/Novella<br/><br/>Wow! What a hot, fun, charming surprise this was! <br/><br/>Two strangers...a tattooed, pierced, skull trimmed, scarred hero who’s all rugged bad boy on the outside (think Zsadist look alike) and sweet, considerate, vulnerable teddy bear gentleman on the inside and a smart, funny, understanding, and genuine heroine...discover and explore a deep connection and explosive sexual attraction while stuck together in an elevator. The pitch-black darkness hides their physical</span>
  <span id="freeText14382065105596110892" style="display:none">5 stars – Contemporary Romance/Novella<br /><br />Wow! What a hot, fun, charming surprise this was! <br /><br />Two strangers...a tattooed, pierced, skull trimmed, scarred hero who’s all rugged bad boy on the outside (think Zsadist look alike) and sweet, considerate, vulnerable teddy bear gentleman on the inside and a smart, funny, understanding, and genuine heroine...discover and explore a deep connection and explosive sexual attraction while stuck together in an elevator. The pitch-black darkness hides their physical imperfections and insecurities, which allows them to express themselves emotionally and achieve true intimacy without fear of rejection. But will their sizzling chemistry and soulful closeness remain once they’re back in the light? <br /> <br />Caden and Makenna are delightful characters, and the author does a wonderful job, despite the shorter length, depicting a convincing attachment between them. It’s a great story that I really enjoyed, especially yummy, sweet Caden! 5 stars!<br /><br />And the studtastic cover hunk is a perfect match for Caden! <i>*fans self*</i><br /><br /></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3099666-buggy?shelf=scars-r-sexy">scars-r-sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3099666-buggy?shelf=tattooed-hero">tattooed-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3099666-buggy?shelf=lit-boyfriend">lit-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3099666-buggy?shelf=shelf-12">shelf-12</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3099666-buggy?shelf=contemp-rom">contemp-rom</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3099666-buggy?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3099666-buggy?shelf=quickie">quickie</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer218996320" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11560442158674432358">Opening Line: <i>" Wait! Can you please hold that?"</i><br/><br/>Ah Caden, my new literary boyfriend, how I would love to get stuck in an elevator with you. Pierced, tattooed, skull trimmed and hitting all my Zsadist fantasy buttons (gah) this bad boy had me in bits from page one. He’s also kind, insecure, lonely and somewhat tortured. Yup he's delicious.<br/><br/>Wow, this was a fantastic little read that I can see myself coming back to again soon. Short, sexy and just oh so good. The only thing that could have made this</span>
  <span id="freeText11560442158674432358" style="display:none">Opening Line: <i>" Wait! Can you please hold that?"</i><br /><br />Ah Caden, my new literary boyfriend, how I would love to get stuck in an elevator with you. Pierced, tattooed, skull trimmed and hitting all my Zsadist fantasy buttons (gah) this bad boy had me in bits from page one. He’s also kind, insecure, lonely and somewhat tortured. Yup he's delicious.<br /><br />Wow, this was a fantastic little read that I can see myself coming back to again soon. Short, sexy and just oh so good. The only thing that could have made this any better would have been a couple hundred more pages. Although in saying that this is perfectly complete in terms of story and unlike most novellas I never felt that our couple’s sexy time was contrived or rushed. I just enjoyed them so much I wanted more. Always the sign of a great story.<br /><br />Makenna as our lucky heroine wasn’t quite what I was expecting; despite her polished appearance and upper class job she had just as many insecurities as Caden did. Will he like what I look like? Will he think I’m homely? Will he want to see me again? This is what every girl thinks and made her relatable and much easier to insert myself into her psyche for fantasy purposes later on.<br /><br />One of the things I really enjoyed here was how the author gave us the exact same moment from both POV’s. Backtracking a conversation or action so that we could get the other persons internal thoughts and reactions to it. I’ve rarely seen this done before and it was awesome to get both sides. I mean how often are you left wondering how he/she feels and you’re stuck in the wrong head? <br /><br />One of my other favourite moments (and this is spoilery) is when Makenna finally gets to see Caden. She exclaims “You’re freaking gorgeous.” I loved this because up until the lights went on we (the readers) didn’t really know what he looked like either. Of course looks are always subjective but I had thought this was going to be beauty and the beast type story, whereas it was more like if The Voice did a dating show. (LOL that made me laugh)Cheers<br /><br /><i>“Tell me, Red, you gotta say it out loud. I can’t see your face or your eyes, and I don’t want to make any mistakes here.”</i><br /><br /><br />-Thanks for the recommendation Tamster<br />290jb5</span>
  <a data-text-id="11560442158674432358" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer17469017562151865663">This wasn’t like xxx or anything, it was sexy though. Caden and Mckena meet in an elevator, the chemistry was perfect between them. The sparks flew. Caden definitely has a bad boy look, while she has a polished pit together look. Caden definitely has his issues, while they both have experienced loss. Their connection is fast, but it seems to be the norm in a lot of books. It was a quick read, that I enjoyed.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer171842706" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8438499190009437145"><br/>When total strangers, Caden Grayson and Makenna James, end up stuck together in an elevator that breaks down, somehow there in that pitch black box, they’re able to see more of each other than if they had met on a bright, sunny day. And who knows? Had they met under any other circumstances, appearances would probably have kept them apart but with nothing to get in the way, this seemingly conservative businesswoman and this scarred, tattooed paramedic have to rely on their other senses to get to </span>
  <span id="freeText8438499190009437145" style="display:none"><br />When total strangers, Caden Grayson and Makenna James, end up stuck together in an elevator that breaks down, somehow there in that pitch black box, they’re able to see more of each other than if they had met on a bright, sunny day. And who knows? Had they met under any other circumstances, appearances would probably have kept them apart but with nothing to get in the way, this seemingly conservative businesswoman and this scarred, tattooed paramedic have to rely on their other senses to get to know one another. When I read a story like <i>Hearts in Darkness,</i> I can actually believe that sometimes fate will step in and help two lost souls find one another.<br /><br />This is a short, very hot story that had a satisfying <i>happy for now</i> ending, one that made me believe Caden and Makenna would eventually get a <i>happily ever after</i> ending, too.<br /><br />Thanks for bringing this wonderful book to my attention, Juliana, and for encouraging me to read this, NOW, Baba! I really, really enjoyed it!<br /><br /></span>

          </span>

    <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy"><img alt="Stacey is Sassy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474185067p2/12062194.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/396576104?book_show_action=true">Aug 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey is Sassy" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy">Stacey is Sassy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/11258847-hearts-in-darkness">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer396576104" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2610858705298023310"><strong>Good Sam and Red meet in the dark</strong><br/><br/>This was a re-read for me and I loved it as much as the first time I read it. Hearts in Darkness is intense, thoughtful and beautifully put together story in a little package. I have only read one other short story that left me so thoroughly entertained.<br/><br/>Makenna had a rough day that got even worse when her phone broke and she realised that the battery had fallen out. Caden, had just signed the final papers after his Dad had passed. He holds the lift for her. He no</span>
  <span id="freeText2610858705298023310" style="display:none"><strong>Good Sam and Red meet in the dark</strong><br><br>This was a re-read for me and I loved it as much as the first time I read it. Hearts in Darkness is intense, thoughtful and beautifully put together story in a little package. I have only read one other short story that left me so thoroughly entertained.<br><br>Makenna had a rough day that got even worse when her phone broke and she realised that the battery had fallen out. Caden, had just signed the final papers after his Dad had passed. He holds the lift for her. He noticed her beautiful red hair and she noticed a sexy tattoo. That was all...and then there was darkness.<br><br>Their time together in the lift gives them the opportunity to know each other without the pressures and judgments based on looks. Both are concerned that something in their looks would put the other off. How amazing that they were given this opportunity. Unfortunately as a society, we put a lot of pressure on ourselves and others based purely on looks. This book took that away. Lucky for them, they liked the packaging too.<br><br>This was a very HOT read and left me with a big smile on my face. This is a perfect example of what a short story should be.<br><br><a href="http://staceyissassy.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440643271i/16004133._SX540_.jpg" width="300" height="48" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/Sassyreviews" rel="nofollow noopener"> <span>[image error]</span></a></span>

          </span>

<div id="review_1316981079" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1316981079" />
    <a title="Natalie ✩★ The Biblioholic ★✩" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic"><img alt="Natalie ✩★ The Biblioholic ★✩" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529028941p2/39243185.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1316981079?book_show_action=true">Sep 02, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natalie ✩★ The Biblioholic ★✩" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natalie ✩★ The Biblioholic ★✩" href="/user/show/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic">Natalie ✩★ The Biblioholic ★✩</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18137628-hearts-in-darkness">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic?shelf=2020">2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1316981079" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16697536972377012750">Can you imagine being stuck in the dark, in an elevator, with a complete stranger? What if they're not a good person? What if they stink? Makenna and Caden were fortunate to be stuck with one other. They learned about each other with no preconceptions. No distractions. No worrying if the other person was attractive or if they found you attractive. No wondering if they said too much. They grew close, closer than most people, in the span of hours. Makenna knew more about Caden than she knew about </span>
  <span id="freeText16697536972377012750" style="display:none">Can you imagine being stuck in the dark, in an elevator, with a complete stranger? What if they're not a good person? What if they stink? Makenna and Caden were fortunate to be stuck with one other. They learned about each other with no preconceptions. No distractions. No worrying if the other person was attractive or if they found you attractive. No wondering if they said too much. They grew close, closer than most people, in the span of hours. Makenna knew more about Caden than she knew about most people in her life. Caden grew attached to Makenna in a way he couldn't be to anyone else.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>Caden couldn't remember the last time he'd had such an easy conversation or the last time he'd laughed or even smiled so much.</b>
</blockquote><br /><br />I really enjoyed this story. I liked it so much, from beginning to end, that I don't even feel it necessary to read the next book in this duet. I probably will because it will give me more of these characters and the future that they have together, but I don't need to. This author captured such a unique experience in a wonderfully sweet way. I couldn't help but be captivated by this story.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16697536972377012750" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_171854694" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/171854694" />
    <a title="Auntee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/886675-auntee"><img alt="Auntee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1281897695p2/886675.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/171854694?book_show_action=true">May 28, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Auntee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Auntee" href="/user/show/886675-auntee">Auntee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/11258847-hearts-in-darkness">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of erotic short stories</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Auntee by: </span>
      Shawna
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=for_my_kindle">for_my_kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=e-books">e-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=anthologies-novellas">anthologies-novellas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=where-s-my-epilogue">where-s-my-epilogue</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=2013_reads">2013_reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer171854694" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17307395957619359318"><b>This is how you write an erotic short story!</b><br/><br/>Wow. This little gem had me hooked from the start. Harried red haired young businesswoman Makenna is having a rough day where everything seems to be going wrong. Luckily a good Samaritan (with a tattooed hand) is holding the elevator door open for her... no sooner does the door close and before Makenna can get a clear look at her "Good Sam", the elevator shudders to a halt and the lights go out. Uh-oh. It just so happens that the tattooed stranger (an </span>
  <span id="freeText17307395957619359318" style="display:none"><b>This is how you write an erotic short story!</b><br><br>Wow. This little gem had me hooked from the start. Harried red haired young businesswoman Makenna is having a rough day where everything seems to be going wrong. Luckily a good Samaritan (with a tattooed hand) is holding the elevator door open for her... no sooner does the door close and before Makenna can get a clear look at her "Good Sam", the elevator shudders to a halt and the lights go out. Uh-oh. It just so happens that the tattooed stranger (an EMT named Caden) is claustrophobic and has a fear of dark places...What will happen when these two strangers are trapped for who knows how long?<br><br><i>Caden...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/books/750513f1-3073-4858-8e8c-a58a331e417b_zps7090ffd4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380350593i/704347.jpg" alt=" photo 750513f1-3073-4858-8e8c-a58a331e417b_zps7090ffd4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Makenna...</i><br><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/books/0d2367f8-b02c-4435-a6e6-dde3639b3a59_zps74347038.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380350593i/704348.jpg" alt=" photo 0d2367f8-b02c-4435-a6e6-dde3639b3a59_zps74347038.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>I loved it! Usually with this premise it's the hero who has to take care of and calm the heroine down, so I loved that this was all switched around. I love me a dangerous-looking hero (Caden was pierced, scarred, and tattooed) who's a real softie inside. I love when the hero has some emotional issues that the heroine can help him overcome. <i>I love a vulnerable hero, who's unsure of his attractiveness!</i> Caden was all this! And I loved Makenna too. She was smart, funny, and understanding, and just a bit unsure of herself too. I loved how the author threw them together in this situation, but had them really get to know one another first (loved the dialogue) before they let the mutual attraction take over. And I like how they were attracted to each other without either having a clear picture of what the other looked like. Loved how the sexual tension built and built before we got the big payoff--<i>super steamy</i>!<br><br>What would've made this erotic quickie perfect? <i>An epilogue!</i> Oh where oh where was the epilogue?? I'm dying to know what happened with these two! Oh well, I guess if your readers are left begging for more, you've written a winner. I hope one day Laura Kaye does us a favor and revisits these characters--there's so much more I'd like to know! 4 1/2 stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="17307395957619359318" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1466530352" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1466530352" />
    <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog"><img alt="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554795448p2/3870376.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1466530352?book_show_action=true">Dec 11, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog">Jenny - TotallybookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1466530352" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16880174811001210536"><b> Re-Read </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452613921i/17717205._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Joint review for Heart in Darkness (re-read) & Love in the Light. <br/><br/><i>“I will fight for you until you can fight for yourself.”</i></b><br/><br/>We decided to re-read Hearts in Darkness as we read it back in 2011 pre-blog days therefore never reviewed this 5 star read. Also it’s one of our favourite stories as well as couples so we wanted the full impact. This sequel has been one we’ve wished for with all our hearts as we’ve never forgotten Caden and Makenna. We wanted to hear what happened after that fateful</span>
  <span id="freeText16880174811001210536" style="display:none"><b> Re-Read </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452613921i/17717205._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Joint review for Heart in Darkness (re-read) &amp; Love in the Light. <br><br><i>“I will fight for you until you can fight for yourself.”</i></b><br><br>We decided to re-read Hearts in Darkness as we read it back in 2011 pre-blog days therefore never reviewed this 5 star read. Also it’s one of our favourite stories as well as couples so we wanted the full impact. This sequel has been one we’ve wished for with all our hearts as we’ve never forgotten Caden and Makenna. We wanted to hear what happened after that fateful day they ended up stuck together in an elevator for four hours. We wanted that intensity and emotionally laden moment back.<br><br><b>‘The darkness combined with the intensity of their connection made her feel like nothing else existed in the world. She’d never experienced this kind of passion before – at least not from a kiss alone.’</b><br><br>Two strangers – a brief glimpse before they’re plunged into darkness. A man with demons after a tragic childhood, a woman with a huge heart who loves with everything she has. It was intense, it was all encompassing. It was where two souls found each other knowing they were home. Two opposites in almost every way yet they fit perfectly!<br><br><b>‘What Caden did mattered to a lot of people. Which meant that he mattered, whether he felt it or not.’</b><br><br>We just loved being back with Makenna and Caden, experiencing that first moment they connected and felt every emotion and passion once more before diving straight into Love in the Light.<br><br><b>‘She didn’t love him despite of all his issues, she loved him because of them. Or, rather, because they were part of who he was. And she loved who he was. With everything she had.’</b><br><br>Makenna is one of our favourite heroines out there. She’s settled and happy in life despite losing her mother at an early age. Her protective brothers and her loving Father make her life complete and with a strong and mature head on her shoulders she embraces her heart and wants knowing it’s Caden she wants and desires despite what may prove to be a bumpy ride. She’s in it one hundred percent and she never wavers.<br><br><b>‘Hey, lightening, let me show you what I really care about so you know where to strike next.’</b><br><br>We have to say that we fell even more in love with our feisty red head in this sequel. She showed incredible compassion, trust, understanding and above all others – love.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Then it’s you and me, ‘til the end. In the darkness and in the light.”</i>
</b><br><br>Caden…what can we say, he was one of our first book boyfriends as we fell for this beautiful damaged man who’d turned his life around but still wasn’t complete nor at peace with himself after the trauma and tragedy he’s been through at such an early age. We wholeheartedly love him and fancy the bloody pants off of this man. In Makenna’s words:<br><br><b>
  <i>“You are so freaking gorgeous and so smoking hot that you make my mouth water and my panties melt. Every time I see you.”</i>
</b><br><br>This was fundamentally his story as he comes to terms with his past and makes peace with it realising his own worth and role in life.<br><br><b>‘He’d stopped trusting her…not to abandon him….He’d made his own worst fears come true.’</b><br><br>Reading these two books together was really quite an emotional journey despite what we already knew. Laura Kaye really wrote something so very special here that will stay in our loving book hearts forever. We highly recommend you pick these up if you’ve not already met our Caden and Makenna. You will never regret this journey full of emotion, passion, twists and inspirational moments.<br><br><b>
  <i>“You’re all big heart and kind soul. And don’t ever change.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452613921i/17717206._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>♥ ♥ ♥<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409751100i/11016560._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Come say hi and follow us at:<br>✦ <a href="http://totallybookedblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">TotallybookedBlog</a><br>✦ <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/TotallyBooked/257135974397181%20&lt;br%20/&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Facebook</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/TotallyBooked1%20&lt;/b&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Twitter</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/totallybookedb/" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Pinterest</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="16880174811001210536" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_180200329" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/180200329" />
    <a title="Juliana Philippa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1378820-juliana-philippa"><img alt="Juliana Philippa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597182219p2/1378820.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/180200329?book_show_action=true">Jun 27, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Juliana Philippa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Juliana Philippa" href="/user/show/1378820-juliana-philippa">Juliana Philippa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18137628-hearts-in-darkness">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Lovers of amazing gruff/sweet heroes, opposites attract, great chemistry, unusual circumstances</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1378820-juliana-philippa?shelf=2011-reads">2011-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1378820-juliana-philippa?shelf=4-to-5-stars">4-to-5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1378820-juliana-philippa?shelf=cr-hero-motorcycle-tattoo-bad-boy">cr-hero-motorcycle-tattoo-bad-boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1378820-juliana-philippa?shelf=0-own">0-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1378820-juliana-philippa?shelf=cr-heroine-somewhat-wallflower">cr-heroine-somewhat-wallflower</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1378820-juliana-philippa?shelf=cr-sizzling-chemistry">cr-sizzling-chemistry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1378820-juliana-philippa?shelf=2011-reads-my-favorites-of-the-year">2011-reads-my-favorites-of-the-year</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1378820-juliana-philippa?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1378820-juliana-philippa?shelf=0-this-is-main-gr-edition">0-this-is-main-gr-edition</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1378820-juliana-philippa?shelf=0-reviewed">0-reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer180200329" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11516802587809085289"><i>Reread February 6, 2016:</i> changed rating from 4.5 to 4; wanted to reread it before I read the next book!<br/><br/><b>Not normally a novella fan and didn't have high expectations, but ended up *loving* it <i>(4.5 stars)</i></b><br/>I absolutely loved this novella (and like most, only wish it was longer!). Short romances almost invariably get bad ratings from me, because I'm unable to believe any lasting connection, but in this case I had no trouble with that. I found the idea of this new relationship fully believable and whol</span>
  <span id="freeText11516802587809085289" style="display:none"><i>Reread February 6, 2016:</i> changed rating from 4.5 to 4; wanted to reread it before I read the next book!<br /><br /><b>Not normally a novella fan and didn't have high expectations, but ended up *loving* it <i>(4.5 stars)</i></b><br />I absolutely loved this novella (and like most, only wish it was longer!). Short romances almost invariably get bad ratings from me, because I'm unable to believe any lasting connection, but in this case I had no trouble with that. I found the idea of this new relationship fully believable and wholly enjoyable - and much sweeter than I expected.<br /><br /><b>{ Hero }</b><br />Caden was such a fantastic hero. He's big and buff, tattooed, has piercings and a shaved head - if you saw him walking towards you in a dark alley you'd think twice about staying there - however he's one of those absolutely teddy bear heroes that's gruff on the outside but a softie inside (he works as an EMT). A lot of times those types of heroes are gruff to everyone until the heroine breaks him down, but here Caden's only "gruffness" is really <i>only</i> his outer appearance. He's actually quiet and somewhat shy, and I loved how sometimes he was tentative and vulnerable, not sure how he should act with her or how far to go, and other times he was so passionate and possessive. From the beginning he's very sweet and kind towards Makenna, which I loved.<br /><br /><b>{ Heroine }</b><br />Makenna was a great heroine, but I actually didn't feel like I knew her as well as I did Caden by the end of the book. When we're with Caden's POV, I feel like we get much more insight into his personality, thoughts, and insecurities than we do for Makenna when we're with her POV. I liked her though, and I'm often tougher on heroines than heroes. She's hard-working, intelligent, sweet, and has a good sense of humor. She's used to being considered one of the guys and while not supremely confident about her attractions, she's definitely not insecure - which from other people's comments/shelving had been what I was expecting.<br /><br /><b>{ The Romance }</b><br />Honestly, I was not going into this with high expectations. I thought I would probably find the whole thing somewhat sleazy if these two people who don't know one another get stuck in a dark elevator with each other and then have sex (for those worried about this as well: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[they don't sleep with one another in the elevator, but after <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>). Basically, I wasn't sure how much of a "romance" this would actually be, but I was very pleasantly surprised. Normally I hate - <b>hate!</b> - instant attraction, one night stand romances, etc., but none of that felt like it was part of this story. <br /><br />There is <i>definite</i> chemistry between the two and Kaye writes wonderful sexual tension, but I felt like they did get to know one another and certainly had an emotional/intellectual connection as well; I loved the conversation between them and their back and forth banter. They can't see one another, so while they're intrigued by the little they did notice about one another before the lights went out (her red hair, his tattoos), that's not the basis of how they start their relationship. I think the fact that they're in the dark allows both of them to let their guard down from the beginning much more than they might otherwise. It also allows them to look beyond the outer appearance - Caden, the big, scary guy and Makenna, the boring accountant.<br /><br /><b>{ Criticisms }</b><br />One of the most annoying things throughout the book was that there were no space breaks between POV transitions. It made it so that each time the POV switched I wouldn't really realize it until the end of the first or second paragraph; minor complaint, but since it could have been so easily fixed it bugged me all the more. Also didn't like how the transitions would rehash what had just happened but from the other character's POV. Other than that, I had a little eye-rolling towards the end when Makenna offers her interpretation of what Caden uses his tattoos for and he has this shocked oh-my-god-this-woman-can-see-right-into-my-soul reaction. Again, minor, but this book was so great I don't have any major complaints to share!<br /><br /><b>{ Bottom Line }</b><br />As unusual as the circumstances of them meeting are, the entire encounter - and what follows - felt realistic, as if I could meet these two people and completely believe that they met that way and were still together. Their conversations were cute and funny, their thoughts and feelings sweet, and their chemistry was sizzling. All in all, a perfect novella and one I am so glad that I bought! Laura Kaye is a brand new author whom I hadn't heard of before, but I will now <i>definitely</i> be keeping my eyes out for her future work.<br /><br /><b>{ Recommendations }</b><br />* <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/878000.Wanting_What_You_Get__Stepp_Sisters_Trilogy___2_" title="Wanting What You Get (Stepp Sisters Trilogy, #2) by Kathy Love" rel="nofollow noopener">Wanting What You Get</a>
</i> by Kathy Love (5 stars)<br />* <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11084987.Negligee_Behavior" title="Negligee Behavior by Shelli Stevens" rel="nofollow noopener">Negligee Behavior</a>
</i> by Shelli Stevens (4.5 stars)<br />* <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5841508.One_Reckless_Summer__Destiny___1_" title="One Reckless Summer (Destiny, #1) by Toni Blake" rel="nofollow noopener">One Reckless Summer</a>
</i> by Toni Blake (4.5 stars)<br />* <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8379666.Whisper_Falls__Destiny___3_" title="Whisper Falls (Destiny, #3) by Toni Blake" rel="nofollow noopener">Whisper Falls</a>
</i> by Toni Blake (4.5 stars)<br />* <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5818483.The_Sweetest_Tattoo__Cabin_Fever___1_" title="The Sweetest Tattoo (Cabin Fever, #1) by Cameron Dane" rel="nofollow noopener">The Sweetest Tattoo</a>
</i> by Cameron Dane (4 stars)<br />* <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/620385.Lead_Me_On__Pearl_Island_Trilogy___2_" title="Lead Me On (Pearl Island Trilogy, #2) by Julie Ortolon" rel="nofollow noopener">Lead Me On</a>
</i> by Julie Ortolon (4 stars)<br /><br /><i>(Written June 27, 2011)</i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2490447381912041497">Aw, this was a lovely, sweet and very hot little novella.<br/><br/>It's about 2 people in an elevator who never get a proper look at each other before the lights go out and the elevator breaks down. They are, outwardly, 2 very different people - Makenna is a suit-wearing accountant and Caden is a tattooed, pierced paramedic. Without the benefit of sight to give them pre-conceived ideas, they get to know one another in the darkness, realising they have plenty in common, and there is an undeniable physical </span>
  <span id="freeText2490447381912041497" style="display:none">Aw, this was a lovely, sweet and very hot little novella.<br /><br />It's about 2 people in an elevator who never get a proper look at each other before the lights go out and the elevator breaks down. They are, outwardly, 2 very different people - Makenna is a suit-wearing accountant and Caden is a tattooed, pierced paramedic. Without the benefit of sight to give them pre-conceived ideas, they get to know one another in the darkness, realising they have plenty in common, and there is an undeniable physical attraction between them which is all chemistry and nothing to do with their appearances.<br /><br />Definitely going to seek out more by this author.<br /><br /></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940012668929" href="/book/show/11201007-hearts-in-darkness">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=hawt-protectors-fbi-army-cops">hawt-protectors-fbi-army-cops</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=sexy-as-fuck">sexy-as-fuck</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=broken">broken</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=favourties">favourties</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=re-reads">re-reads</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer562745156" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9580697078287037937"><b>5 <i>"My Good Sam"</i> STARS</b><br/><br/><i>"Love looks not with the eyes, but with the mind; and therefore is winged Cupid painted blind."</i> ~ William Shakespeare<br/><br/>There are so many things I love about this novella. I think first and foremost is the fact that two people, Caden and Mackenna, form a bond - a strong, sizzling connection - without really setting eyes on each other. Like the quote above says, it just speaks to the beauty of the mind and heart to find love without looks to distort the reality. <br/><br/>This is also one</span>
  <span id="freeText9580697078287037937" style="display:none"><b>5 <i>"My Good Sam"</i> STARS</b><br /><br /><i>"Love looks not with the eyes, but with the mind; and therefore is winged Cupid painted blind."</i> ~ William Shakespeare<br /><br />There are so many things I love about this novella. I think first and foremost is the fact that two people, Caden and Mackenna, form a bond - a strong, sizzling connection - without really setting eyes on each other. Like the quote above says, it just speaks to the beauty of the mind and heart to find love without looks to distort the reality. <br /><br />This is also one hot read. This is seriously a sexual fantasy come true. Imagine being stuck in an elevator for hours in the dark with a big, muscular man who speaks his mind, is gentle with his ways, sweet with his words and smells delicious...*shakes my head and sighs* sorry, back to my review...Their time trapped in the elevator is one utterly mouthwatering (among other things) tease!! <br /><br /><b>"I love that elevator."</b><br /><br />I'm super excited to see what happens with Caden and Mackenna. I've been waiting a long time for this. If you're looking for an original and scorching hot quick read with the potential for so much more, you must read this!!<br />-----------------------------------------<br /><b>re-reading this in anticipation of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25396316.Love_in_the_Light__Hearts_in_Darkness___2_" title="Love in the Light (Hearts in Darkness, #2) by Laura Kaye" rel="nofollow noopener">Love in the Light</a> that comes out this Tuesday. FINALLY!!<br /><br />Release Tuesday, January 12th<br />Amazon: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1RBk1YG">http://amzn.to/1RBk1YG</a></b><br /><br />First read March 2012</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17791942533895098044">Oh.My.Goodness!!! and YUM!! <i>Sinfully</i> smexy!! Definitely not a YA!<br/><br/>Mackenna has had a long day and can think of nothing better than going home and having a big glass of wine. She's about to miss the elevator and being a nice guy, Caden holds the door for her. Mackenna, preoccupied with holding all of her bags and cell phone, only catches a glimpse of this guy's tattooed arm before the power goes out and the elevator stops. Caden for his part doesn't see anything of Mackenna except for her long red</span>
  <span id="freeText17791942533895098044" style="display:none">Oh.My.Goodness!!! and YUM!! <i>Sinfully</i> smexy!! Definitely not a YA!<br /><br />Mackenna has had a long day and can think of nothing better than going home and having a big glass of wine. She's about to miss the elevator and being a nice guy, Caden holds the door for her. Mackenna, preoccupied with holding all of her bags and cell phone, only catches a glimpse of this guy's tattooed arm before the power goes out and the elevator stops. Caden for his part doesn't see anything of Mackenna except for her long red hair, and professional grey suit. <br /><br />So now they are stuck in the elevator together, which is bad news for Caden. He is claustrophobic and is having a hard time until Mackenna starts talking to him. They start playing twenty-questions and talk about everything, and from there the attraction starts to build. <br /><br />This story was a lot of fun, a quick read, and boy was there a lot of smexy *blushes thinking about it*! It is only 112 pages(according to Amazon, this site says 230??) and the pages just flew by. I loved how these two got to know each other and how sight unseen they were attracted. This is my second time reading this (I was reading something else and got distracted!) and I really, really liked it, so I felt I should come back and give it a proper review! <br /> <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17791942533895098044" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14379473-leila?shelf=broken-hero">broken-hero</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1375088794" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8097803096544849829"><b>4 claustrophobic stars!</b><br/><br/>What an interesting concept for a story. Two strangers, trapped in an elevator overnight, in complete and total darkness. This was a wonderful story of two people coming together to get themselves through a tough situation.<br/><br/>Neither Caden nor MaKenna got a good look at each other when they stepped into that fated elevator. All MaKenna knew was that her Good Samaritan, Caden, had tattoos on his hands and arms. All Caden saw of MaKenna was her fiery red hair and cute bottom.<br/><br/>I </span>
  <span id="freeText8097803096544849829" style="display:none"><b>4 claustrophobic stars!</b><br /><br />What an interesting concept for a story. Two strangers, trapped in an elevator overnight, in complete and total darkness. This was a wonderful story of two people coming together to get themselves through a tough situation.<br /><br />Neither Caden nor MaKenna got a good look at each other when they stepped into that fated elevator. All MaKenna knew was that her Good Samaritan, Caden, had tattoos on his hands and arms. All Caden saw of MaKenna was her fiery red hair and cute bottom.<br /><br />I loved that these two characters connected on such a deeper level because they couldn’t pass that initial judgement on looks. As the night wears on their conversation becomes more serious and the heart connection grows intimately deeper. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Peace was not an emotion with which he was much familiar, but with MaKenna he had it. And he didn’t know how he was going to ever give it up.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />I wish going into this book I had known that it was just a short novella. It left me wanting for so much more of a story than what was given, though I was spellbound by it from beginning to end.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14178834579819308574"><b><u>This was a buddy read with the gorgeous Rain</u><br/>Recommended by the lovely Sarah and Rain<3</b><br/><br/><b>I'll be honest right from the start. At one time this book would have been a <u>5 STAR</u> book as it has a sexy man with <br><br>Tattoo's<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395554i/761886.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and a gorgeous face complete with biteable lip piercings <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395554i/761887.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But recently I have got into m/m books and darker reads so I won't say too much about this book as I don't think it is fair to put people off a truly fantastic book. And she wanted to get to know both sides a lot better'<br><br>'Now that Makenna had a source of friction, she had to use it. She ground herself against his considerable hardness and whimpered at how good he felt, there'</i></blockquote>

<div id="review_2069071691" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="bella farren" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23223005-bella-farren"><img alt="bella farren" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598064440p2/23223005.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2069071691?book_show_action=true">Jul 23, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="bella farren" class="user" itemprop="url" name="bella farren" href="/user/show/23223005-bella-farren">bella farren</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23223005-bella-farren?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23223005-bella-farren?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2069071691" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17766564583168507711"><b>2/5 stars</b><br/><br/>Supremely disappointed with this one, it felt like a bit of a cop out that the contents of what should be one story, has been split across two books.<br/><br/>This book literally spans four hours, of which time they’re basically locked in an elevator the whole time. I can understand how some books only span a day, and are packed full of events and exciting moments, but this was the single most monotonous book I’ve read. <br/><br/>Nothing exciting can really happen while two people are locked in an elevator</span>
  <span id="freeText17766564583168507711" style="display:none"><b>2/5 stars</b><br /><br />Supremely disappointed with this one, it felt like a bit of a cop out that the contents of what should be one story, has been split across two books.<br /><br />This book literally spans four hours, of which time they’re basically locked in an elevator the whole time. I can understand how some books only span a day, and are packed full of events and exciting moments, but this was the single most monotonous book I’ve read. <br /><br />Nothing exciting can really happen while two people are locked in an elevator. <b>They spoke. They ate the little food and water they had on them. They spoke. They hooked up. They got out. They hooked up again. Finished. </b><br /><br />This book felt like the beginning of books where you have to push through a backstory dump, too much dialog and the boring scenes of characters meeting before you get to the good stuff. But you know, without the good stuff. <br /><br />I found the character dialog and backstories interesting enough but it didn’t captivate me. I was left feeling like the story was lacking in emotional pull and there was no real plot lines to speak of. I didn’t mind the character chemistry but again, there wasn’t enough of the book for me to feel a real connection with the characters. <br /><br />I’m irritated that I finished this book in about half an hour and it’s priced as a full ebook (imo). I read the sample for the next book and it seems to be about them meeting family and trying to have a relationship, the two books should have been condensed into one actual sized book with a plot line. <br /><br />Definitely won’t be buying the next one.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17766564583168507711" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('wHF00YDPxf0CsxmRwAdVwafWDON9O4o8PUHjTXnB/UeHKFMN0rRdOcQY3EkJJL7rQU+Gp5K32VgiTMQYM98GZg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('5z4PDBSHIEmARhtBB7lFZllzGEWaEt/C801SILcsKC+gZyjQRvy4jUbt3pnOmq5Mv+qSAXWejKbsQHV1/TLTDg==')})
  }
//]]>

  <span id="freeText168978643743563327" style="display:none">Laura Kaye is the New York Times and USA Today Bestselling author of contemporary and erotic romance and romantic suspense, including the Hard Ink, Raven Riders, Blasphemy, Heroes, and Hearts of the Anemoi series. Laura's hot, heartfelt stories are all about the universal desire for a place to belong. Laura grew up amidst family lore involving angels, ghosts, and evil-eye curses, cementing her life-long fascination with storytelling and the supernatural. Laura also writes historical fiction as Laura Kamoie, and lives in Maryland with her husband and two daughters, and appreciates her view of the Chesapeake Bay every day.<br /><br />Join Laura Kaye's Newsletter - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smarturl.it/subscribeLauraKaye">smarturl.it/subscribeLauraKaye</a> - to Receive:<br /><br />*New release alerts *News about contests and giveaways *Sneak peeks and teasers *Early cover reveals *The most up-to-date book news and new releases *Book signings and appearances *Online events for readers *Upcoming sales</span>
